necessary to be successful at Rose-Hulman; and guiding them in the

Sedentary

their ability to learn.

your advisees towards experiences that will enable them to learn

graduation or (b) help them to advance in their future career.

Q: PH 327 & PH 401 are required for the Engineering Physics degree.

The Core Curriculum of RIT requires students to take a minimum of 12 credits of Humanities and Social Sciences as defined by the Department of Liberal Arts. Additionally, 3 credits of upper level HSSA electives are required. These HSSA electives must be 300 level or higher, and must be chosen from the following departments: Economics, English, History, Modern Languages and Cultures (MLC), Philosophy, Political Science, Science Technology and Society (STS), and Sociology/Anthropology.

The Natural Science Elective must be selected from the following list: BIOL 111, BIOL 112, CHEM 111, CHEM 112, CHEM 113, ENSC 150, ENSC 201, ENSC 202, ENSC 203, ESCI 101, ESCI 102, ESCI 103, ESCI 104, ESCI 105, ESCI 106, ESCI 107, ESCI 108, ESCI 109, ESCI 110, ESCI 111, ESCI 112, ESCI 113, ESCI 114, ESCI 115, ESC
